        <h1>
         Over 60% of us have had 'disastrous' dates, reveals new survey - from men bringing their moms, to discussions about 'bowel movements'
        </h1>
        <p class="author-section byline-plain">
         By
         <a class="author" href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Annabel+Fenwick+Elliott+for+MailOnline" rel="nofollow">
          Annabel Fenwick Elliott for MailOnline
         </a>
        </p>
        <p class="byline-section">
         <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published">
          <span class="article-timestamp-label">
           Published:
          </span>
          12:30 EST, 11 December 2014
         </span>
         |
         <span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-updated">
          <span class="article-timestamp-label">
           Updated:
          </span>
          12:57 EST, 11 December 2014
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>

        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em">
          Most of us have at least one anecdotal terrible-first-date experience to reel off for comic value, but the following horror stories might just blow yours clean out of the water.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          A survey of 1,000 Americans conducted by activity-booking website
          <a class="" href="http://www.vimbly.com/splash" rel="nofollow" style="font-weight: bold;" target="_blank">
           Vimbly
          </a>
          found that over 63per cent of those asked reported having had 'disastrous' dates; everything from men bringing their moms along to discussing their 'recent bowel movements.'
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          One subject recalls: 'He brought his mother as a chaperone. The entire conversation was about her and how close they were. It went downhill from there. The date started at 8pm. It was over by 8:45pm.'
         </font>
        </p>
        <div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">
         <div class="mol-img">
          <img alt="Check please!A survey of 1,000 Americans conducted by activity-booking website Vimbly found that over 63per cent of those asked reported having had 'disastrous' dates" class="blkBorder img-share" height="423" id="i-a9e8bb3984f0b28" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/pix/2014/12/11/23FA553200000578-0-image-a-9_1418315828025.jpg" width="634"/>
         </div>
         <p class="imageCaption">
          Check please!A survey of 1,000 Americans conducted by activity-booking website Vimbly found that over 63per cent of those asked reported having had 'disastrous' dates
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="art-ins mol-factbox floatLHS femail">
         <h3 class="wocc">
          <b>
           TOP FIVE TURN-OFFS FOR WOMEN
          </b>
         </h3>
         <div class="ins cleared xolcc bdrcc">
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            1. He just wasn't my type
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            2. He was arrogant
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            3. He was rude
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            4. He was unattractive
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            5. He was cheap
           </font>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="art-ins mol-factbox floatLHS femail">
         <h3 class="wocc">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           TOP FIVE TURN-OFFS FOR MEN
          </span>
         </h3>
         <div class="ins cleared xolcc bdrcc">
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            1. She just wasn't my type
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            2. She was rude
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            3. She was selfish
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            4. She was arrogant
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            5. She was unattractive
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
           </font>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Another bad date victim claims her restaurant rendezvous had been going well until another diner recognized her date as having dated both his sister and his mom.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          One woman reported going on a date during which all the man talked about was his dead wife, going as far as to say she was with them in spirit and 'rating' her.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Another man's idea of romantic dinner conversation centered on his 'most recent bowel movement.'
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Then there was the man with some rather unusual anxiety behavior. 'He had a nervous thing where he twisted his hair BUT he had no hair so he was twisting air,' the respondent recalls. 'It was really freaky.'
         </font>
        </p>

         <h3 class="wocc">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           TOP FIVE CONVERSATIONAL TURN-OFFS FOR WOMEN
          </span>
         </h3>
         <div class="ins cleared xolcc bdrcc">
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            1. He only talked about himself
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            2. He didn't say much at all
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            3. He didn't ask any questions
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            4. He only talked about people he knew
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            5. He talked about money
           </font>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="art-ins mol-factbox floatLHS femail">
         <h3 class="wocc">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           TOP FIVE CONVERSATIONAL TURN-OFFS FOR MEN
          </span>
         </h3>
         <div class="ins cleared xolcc bdrcc">
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            1. She didn't say much at all
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            2. She talked about her old boyfriend/spouse
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            3. She only talked about herself
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            4. She didn't ask any questions
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            5. She only talked about people she knew
           </font>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Other epic fails included the man who tried to impress his date with the racy new steering wheel he'd had fitted in his sports car. Catastrophically, the wheel came off in his hands as they were driving along a busy street.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          There was also the tale of the 'awkward 6ft 5in teenager' who found himself a little out of his depth when his date appeared, standing at only 4ft 10in.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          And last but not least, the man lucky enough to get his date back to come home with him, only to then 'load up on trash' and take her to the garbage dump with him.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Vimbly also asked participants, speaking from their various bad date experiences, to list their top turn-offs.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Both men and women stated their number one turn-off was simply that the date 'just wasn't my type.' Women then took issue with men who were 'arrogant, rude, unattractive and cheap' respectively.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Men were most turned off by dates who were 'rude, selfish, arrogant and unattractive'.
         </font>
        </p>

        <div class="art-ins mol-factbox floatLHS femail">
         <h3 class="wocc">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           TOP FIVE BEHAVIORAL NO-NO'S FOR WOMEN
          </span>
         </h3>
         <div class="ins cleared xolcc bdrcc">
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            1. He was too touchy-feely
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            2. He was too serious/depressing
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            3. He drank too much
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            4. He cursed too much
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            5. He was too shy
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
           </font>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="art-ins mol-factbox floatLHS femail">
         <h3 class="wocc">
          <span style="font-weight: bold;">
           TOP FIVE BEHAVIORAL NO-NO'S FOR MEN
          </span>
         </h3>
         <div class="ins cleared xolcc bdrcc">
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em;">
            1. She was too serious/depressing
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            2. She cursed too much
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            3. She was too shy
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            4. She smoked too much
           </font>
          </p>
          <p class="mol-para-with-font">
           <font style="font-size:1.2em">
            5. She was too giddy/excited
           </font>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Interestingly, the top conversational turn-off for women was men who 'only talked about themselves'. For men, it was women who 'didn't say much at all.'
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          The number one behavioral no-no from the women's perspective was men who were 'too touchy-feely.' For men, it was women who were 'too serious/depressing.'
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          And it's not just us mortals who have fallen prey to cringe-inducing first dates.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          Actress Jennifer Love Hewitt once relayed a date she went on with an older man when she was 25. Apparently, the man in question surprised with her an 'N Sync T-Shirt as a gift, then gave her a box of Altoids to 'prep' her for a goodnight kiss.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          British actress Emma Watson told News.com.au last year: 'The worst date Ive ever been on was a guy who told me he couldn't be friends with fat people or anyone who was unattractive. I realized pretty quickly that he was a nutter.'
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size:1.2em">
          And, also last year, TV host Katie Couric told Jimmy Kimmel that she once went on a date with TV personality Larry King, but was forced to 'bolt' after he 'lunged' for a kiss.
         </font>
        </p>
        <p class="mol-para-with-font">
         <font style="font-size: 1.2em">
         </font>
        </p>

       <script async="" src="//cdn.taboola.com/libtrc/dailymail-us/loader.js">
       </script>
       <script type="text/javascript">
        DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '&lt;div id="' + id + '"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;';
            $(node).after(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n});
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=femail&amp;pageSize=10',
            total: 15.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
       </script>
